 succeeded in 817ms:
   1: """Cheap candidate-snippet fetcher feeding the ambiguity detector.
   2: 
   3: Issue I-rdy-009 (#505), Phase 3.6. ``detect_ambiguity`` needs candidate
   4: snippets to cluster, but the dashboard create-run flow has no candidate
   5: source for a *question-only* query (no uploaded documents). Both the
   6: ``ambiguity_detector`` module docstring and the ``/ambiguity`` request
   7: schema named the missing piece:
   8: 
   9:     "Phase 1: backend fetches via cheap retrieval before this call."
  10: 
  11: This module IS that cheap retrieval — a single Serper ``/search`` call
  12: mapped into ``CandidateSnippet`` objects.
  13: 
  14: Why a self-contained Serper call
  15: --------------------------------
  16: The I-rdy-009 brief originally specified reusing ``SerperClient`` from
  17: ``src/search/serper_client.py``. At implement time ``src/search/__init__.py``
  18: was found broken — it imports ``src.search.engines`` and
  19: ``src.search.fan_out_executor``, neither of which exists — so
  20: ``import src.search.serper_client`` raises ``ModuleNotFoundError`` and
  21: ``SerperClient`` is unimportable. This module therefore issues the Serper
  22: ``/search`` request directly via ``httpx``, mirroring the proven pattern
  23: in ``src/polaris_graph/retrieval2/real_fetcher.py`` (slice-002's real
  24: Serper fetcher). Same Serper service, same endpoint, same fail-loud
  25: contract — and no dependency on the broken ``src.search`` package.
  26: 
  27: Fail-loud per CLAUDE.md LAW II
  28: ------------------------------
  29: A missing ``SERPER_API_KEY``, a network/HTTP failure, or a search that
  30: yields zero usable snippets raises ``CandidateFetchError`` rather than
  31: returning an empty list. An empty list would be silently misread by
  32: ``detect_ambiguity`` as "not ambiguous" — the exact false-negative this
  33: guard exists to prevent. Zero results means *search failed*, not *the
  34: question is unambiguous*.
  35: """
  36: 
  37: from __future__ import annotations
  38: 
  39: import os
  40: 
  41: import httpx
  42: 
  43: from polaris_v6.ambiguity_detector.ambiguity_detector import CandidateSnippet
  44: 
  45: SERPER_SEARCH_ENDPOINT = "https://google.serper.dev/search"
  46: DEFAULT_MAX_RESULTS = 10
  47: DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_S = 10.0
  48: 
  49: 
  50: class CandidateFetchError(RuntimeError):
  51:     """Raised when candidate snippets cannot be fetched for a question.
  52: 
  53:     Surfaced by ``POST /ambiguity/scan`` as HTTP 503
  54:     ``candidate_fetch_unavailable`` so the caller fails loud rather than
  55:     proceeding on an empty (falsely-unambiguous) candidate set.
  56:     """
  57: 
  58: 
  59: async def _fetch_serper_organic(
  60:     question: str, *, api_key: str, max_results: int, timeout_s: float
  61: ) -> list[dict]:
  62:     """Issue one Serper ``/search`` request; return the raw ``organic`` list.
  63: 
  64:     Raises ``httpx.HTTPError`` on network failure or a non-2xx response.
  65:     Isolated as a seam so tests can stub the network boundary without
  66:     mocking the detector itself (per CLAUDE.md §9.4).
  67:     """
  68:     payload = {"q": question, "num": max_results}
  69:     headers = {"X-API-KEY": api_key, "Content-Type": "application/json"}
  70:     async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:
  71:         response = await client.post(
  72:             SERPER_SEARCH_ENDPOINT, json=payload, headers=headers, timeout=timeout_s
  73:         )
  74:         response.raise_for_status()
  75:         data = response.json()
  76:     return data.get("organic", []) or []
  77: 
  78: 
  79: async def fetch_candidate_snippets(
  80:     question: str,
  81:     *,
  82:     max_results: int = DEFAULT_MAX_RESULTS,
  83:     timeout_s: float = DEFAULT_TIMEOUT_S,
  84: ) -> list[CandidateSnippet]:
  85:     """Fetch candidate snippets for ``question`` via one cheap web search.
  86: 
  87:     Args:
  88:         question: the user-typed research question.
  89:         max_results: cap on web-search results requested.
  90:         timeout_s: per-request HTTP timeout.
  91: 
  92:     Returns:
  93:         A non-empty list of ``CandidateSnippet`` (``source_id`` = result
  94:         URL, ``text`` = ``"<title>. <snippet>"``).
  95: 
  96:     Raises:
  97:         CandidateFetchError: when ``SERPER_API_KEY`` is unset, the search
  98:             request fails, or it yields zero usable snippets. Never
  99:             returns an empty list — see the module docstring.
 100:     """
 101:     api_key = os.environ.get("SERPER_API_KEY", "").strip()
 102:     if not api_key:
 103:         raise CandidateFetchError(
 104:             "SERPER_API_KEY is unset; cannot fetch ambiguity candidates."
 105:         )
 106: 
 107:     try:
 108:         organic = await _fetch_serper_organic(
 109:             question, api_key=api_key, max_results=max_results, timeout_s=timeout_s
 110:         )
 111:     except httpx.HTTPError as exc:
 112:         raise CandidateFetchError(
 113:             f"Serper web search failed for {question!r}: {exc}"
 114:         ) from exc
 115: 
 116:     snippets: list[CandidateSnippet] = []
 117:     for hit in organic:
 118:         url = hit.get("link", "") or ""
 119:         if not url:
 120:             continue
 121:         title = hit.get("title", "") or ""
 122:         snippet = hit.get("snippet", "") or ""
 123:         text = f"{title}. {snippet}".strip()
 124:         if text in (".", ""):
 125:             # Both title and snippet were empty — nothing to cluster on.
 126:             continue
 127:         snippets.append(CandidateSnippet(source_id=url, text=text))
 128: 
 129:     if not snippets:
 130:         raise CandidateFetchError(
 131:             f"web search returned zero candidate snippets for {question!r}; "
 132:             "the search backend is unreachable or returned no usable results."
 133:         )
 134:     return snippets

 succeeded in 889ms:
   1: """POST /ambiguity — F2 ambiguity check endpoints.
   2: 
   3: Two routes:
   4: 
   5: * ``POST /ambiguity`` — caller supplies candidate snippets directly
   6:   (e.g. the dashboard builds them from uploaded-document chunks).
   7: * ``POST /ambiguity/scan`` (I-rdy-009 / #505) — *question-only*. The
   8:   backend fetches candidate snippets via one cheap web search before
   9:   running ``detect_ambiguity``, so an ambiguous bare question triggers
  10:   the disambiguation modal in the main create-run flow. On a
  11:   candidate-fetch failure it returns HTTP 503
  12:   ``candidate_fetch_unavailable`` — never a silent false-unambiguous
  13:   result.
  14: 
  15: Both return the same ``AmbiguityCheckResponse`` so the frontend can
  16: render a disambiguation modal before any expensive retrieval / generator
  17: cost is incurred.
  18: """
  19: 
  20: from __future__ import annotations
  21: 
  22: from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
  23: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
  24: 
  25: from polaris_v6.ambiguity_detector import (
  26:     CandidateFetchError,
  27:     CandidateSnippet,
  28:     detect_ambiguity,
  29:     fetch_candidate_snippets,
  30: )
  31: from polaris_v6.ambiguity_detector.ambiguity_detector import AmbiguityResult
  32: 
  33: router = APIRouter(prefix="/ambiguity", tags=["ambiguity"])
  34: 
  35: 
  36: class CandidateIn(BaseModel):
  37:     source_id: str
  38:     text: str = Field(..., min_length=1, max_length=8000)
  39: 
  40: 
  41: class AmbiguityCheckRequest(BaseModel):
  42:     question: str = Field(..., min_length=4, max_length=2000)
  43:     candidates: list[CandidateIn] = Field(
  44:         ...,
  45:         min_length=0,
  46:         description=(
  47:             "Pre-fetched candidate snippets. Phase 0: caller supplies. "
  48:             "Phase 1: backend fetches via cheap retrieval before this call."
  49:         ),
  50:     )
  51:     min_cluster_size: int = Field(default=2, ge=1)
  52:     similarity_threshold: float = Field(default=0.5, ge=0.0, le=1.0)
  53: 
  54: 
  55: class AmbiguityScanRequest(BaseModel):
  56:     """POST body for /ambiguity/scan — a question with no caller-supplied
  57:     candidates. The backend fetches candidates itself."""
  58: 
  59:     question: str = Field(..., min_length=4, max_length=2000)
  60: 
  61: 
  62: class AmbiguityClusterOut(BaseModel):
  63:     cluster_id: int
  64:     representative_text: str
  65:     member_source_ids: list[str]
  66: 
  67: 
  68: class AmbiguityCheckResponse(BaseModel):
  69:     is_ambiguous: bool
  70:     clusters: list[AmbiguityClusterOut]
  71:     fallback_used: bool
  72: 
  73: 
  74: def _to_check_response(result: AmbiguityResult) -> AmbiguityCheckResponse:
  75:     """Map a detector ``AmbiguityResult`` onto the HTTP response shape."""
  76:     return AmbiguityCheckResponse(
  77:         is_ambiguous=result.is_ambiguous,
  78:         clusters=[
  79:             AmbiguityClusterOut(
  80:                 cluster_id=c.cluster_id,
  81:                 representative_text=c.representative_text,
  82:                 member_source_ids=c.member_source_ids,
  83:             )
  84:             for c in result.clusters
  85:         ],
  86:         fallback_used=result.fallback_used,
  87:     )
  88: 
  89: 
  90: @router.post("", response_model=AmbiguityCheckResponse)
  91: def check_ambiguity(payload: AmbiguityCheckRequest) -> AmbiguityCheckResponse:
  92:     snippets = [
  93:         CandidateSnippet(source_id=c.source_id, text=c.text) for c in payload.candidates
  94:     ]
  95:     result = detect_ambiguity(
  96:         snippets,
  97:         min_cluster_size=payload.min_cluster_size,
  98:         similarity_threshold=payload.similarity_threshold,
  99:     )
 100:     return _to_check_response(result)
 101: 
 102: 
 103: @router.post("/scan", response_model=AmbiguityCheckResponse)
 104: async def scan_ambiguity(payload: AmbiguityScanRequest) -> AmbiguityCheckResponse:
 105:     """Question-only ambiguity check for the main create-run flow.
 106: 
 107:     Fetches candidate snippets server-side via one cheap web search (the
 108:     "Phase 1" candidate retrieval the ``/ambiguity`` docstring
 109:     anticipated), then runs ``detect_ambiguity``. A candidate-fetch
 110:     failure (no ``SERPER_API_KEY``, search unreachable, zero results)
 111:     returns HTTP 503 ``candidate_fetch_unavailable`` rather than a
 112:     silent false-unambiguous result.
 113:     """
 114:     try:
 115:         snippets = await fetch_candidate_snippets(payload.question)
 116:     except CandidateFetchError as exc:
 117:         raise HTTPException(
 118:             status_code=503,
 119:             detail={
 120:                 "error": True,
 121:                 "code": "candidate_fetch_unavailable",
 122:                 "message": str(exc),
 123:             },
 124:         ) from exc
 125:     result = detect_ambiguity(snippets)
 126:     return _to_check_response(result)

   1: /**
   2:  * POLARIS v6 API client.
   3:  *
   4:  * Mirrors the FastAPI contract in src/polaris_v6/api/{runs,health,stream}.py.
   5:  *
   6:  * I-carney-005 (2026-05-13): all requests are browser-relative paths so the
   7:  * browser only ever talks to the webui origin. Next.js server-side rewrites
   8:  * (web/next.config.ts) forward `/api/v6/*` → `${INTERNAL_API_URL}/*`, which
   9:  * in production compose is `http://api:8000` (a Docker service name the
  10:  * browser cannot resolve directly). In local dev, INTERNAL_API_URL defaults
  11:  * to http://localhost:8000 so `npm run dev` against a host-port-mapped
  12:  * backend works without any client-side configuration.
  13:  *
  14:  * Codex diff iter-1 P1-B: NEXT_PUBLIC_BACKEND_URL is no longer consulted at
  15:  * runtime — baking an absolute http://api:8000 into the client bundle would
  16:  * make production browsers attempt direct Docker-network reach and fail.
  17:  */
  18: 
  19: import { authHeader, redirectToSignIn } from "@/lib/auth";
  20: 
  21: const BACKEND_URL = "/api/v6";
  22: 
  23: /**
  24:  * I-rdy-004 (#500) — fetch wrapper for every v6 API call. Injects the
  25:  * `Authorization: Bearer <jwt>` header, preserves any caller-supplied
  26:  * headers, and does NOT force a content-type (so `FormData` uploads keep
  27:  * their auto-generated multipart boundary). On a 401 it clears the token
  28:  * and routes to /sign-in.
  29:  */
  30: async function authFetch(
  31:   url: string,
  32:   init: RequestInit = {},
  33: ): Promise<Response> {
  34:   const headers = new Headers(init.headers ?? {});
  35:   for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(authHeader())) {
  36:     headers.set(key, value);
  37:   }
  38:   const response = await globalThis.fetch(url, { ...init, headers });
  39:   if (response.status === 401) {
  40:     redirectToSignIn();
  41:   }
  42:   return response;
  43: }
  44: 
  45: /**
  46:  * I-rdy-004 — SSE URL for a run's event stream. Native `EventSource` cannot
  47:  * set request headers, so the JWT rides as the `access_token` query param;
  48:  * the backend `require_auth` accepts it for `/stream/*` paths only.
  49:  */
  50: export function streamUrl(runId: string): string {
  51:   const token = authHeader().Authorization?.replace(/^Bearer /, "");
  52:   const base = `${BACKEND_URL}/stream/${encodeURIComponent(runId)}`;
  53:   return token ? `${base}?access_token=${encodeURIComponent(token)}` : base;
  54: }

  98: async function asJsonOrThrow<T>(response: Response): Promise<T> {
  99:   const body = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 100:   if (!response.ok) {
 101:     const error = new Error(
 102:       `POLARIS backend returned ${response.status}`,
 103:     ) as ApiError;
 104:     error.status = response.status;
 105:     error.body = body;
 106:     throw error;
 107:   }
 108:   return body as T;
 109: }

  86:   );
  87:   const [scopeChecking, setScopeChecking] = useState(false);
  88:   const [uploads, setUploads] = useState<UploadResponse[]>([]);
  89:   const [uploading, setUploading] = useState(false);
  90:   const [dragOver, setDragOver] = useState(false);
  91:   const [ambiguity, setAmbiguity] = useState<AmbiguityResult | null>(null);
  92:   const [acknowledgedAmbiguity, setAcknowledgedAmbiguity] = useState(false);
  93:   const [disambigModalOpen, setDisambigModalOpen] = useState(false);
  94:   const [clinicalScanGate, setClinicalScanGate] = useState<ScanGate>("not_run");
  95:   const [templates, setTemplates] = useState(FALLBACK_TEMPLATES);
  96: 
  97:   // I-rdy-009 (#505): monotonic scan generation. Every scan claims a
  98:   // generation at start; any input edit (invalidateAmbiguityScan) bumps it.
  99:   // An in-flight scan whose generation is stale on resolution discards its
 100:   // result — so a scan started for question A can never set the gate "ok"
 101:   // for an edited-to question B (a ref, so the bump is synchronous and the
 102:   // discard is order-independent of the resolving promise).
 103:   const scanGenerationRef = useRef(0);
 104: 
 105:   useEffect(() => {
 106:     let cancelled = false;
 107:     listTemplates()
 108:       .then((live) => {
 109:         if (!cancelled && live.length > 0) {
 110:           setTemplates(templatesToCards(live));
 111:         }
 112:       })
 113:       .catch(() => {
 114:         // Keep fallback on failure; dashboard still works.
 115:       });
 116:     return () => {
 117:       cancelled = true;
 118:     };
 119:   }, []);
 120: 
 121:   // I-rdy-009 (#505): any change to the question, template, or upload set
 122:   // invalidates a prior ambiguity scan. A stale "ok" gate must not let an
 123:   // edited question reach createRun without its own detect_ambiguity scan.
 124:   // Bumping the generation also cancels any in-flight scan. Called from the
 125:   // question / template / upload event handlers (not an effect — per the
 126:   // react-hooks/set-state-in-effect rule).
 127:   const invalidateAmbiguityScan = () => {
 128:     scanGenerationRef.current += 1;
 129:     setClinicalScanGate("not_run");
 130:     setAmbiguity(null);
 131:     setAcknowledgedAmbiguity(false);
 132:     setDisambigModalOpen(false);
 133:   };
 134: 
 135:   const handleFiles = async (files: FileList | File[]) => {
 136:     const list = Array.from(files);
 137:     if (list.length === 0) return;
 138:     setUploading(true);
 139:     setError(null);
 140:     try {
 141:       const results: UploadResponse[] = [];
 142:       for (const file of list) {
 143:         const result = await uploadDocument(file, "UNKNOWN");
 144:         results.push(result);
 145:       }
 146:       setUploads((prev) => [...prev, ...results]);
 147:       invalidateAmbiguityScan();
 148:     } catch (err) {
 149:       setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Upload failed");
 150:     } finally {
 151:       setUploading(false);
 152:     }
 153:   };
 154: 
 155:   const onDrop = (event: React.DragEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
 156:     event.preventDefault();
 157:     setDragOver(false);
 158:     if (event.dataTransfer.files.length > 0) {
 159:       handleFiles(event.dataTransfer.files);
 160:     }
 161:   };
 162: 
 163:   const runScopeCheck = async () => {
 164:     if (question.trim().length < 1) return;
 165:     // Claim a fresh generation; an edit mid-scan bumps past it and the
 166:     // result-application guards below will discard this scan's output.
 167:     const myGeneration = (scanGenerationRef.current += 1);
 168:     setScopeChecking(true);
 169:     setError(null);
 170:     setAmbiguity(null);
 171:     setAcknowledgedAmbiguity(false);
 172:     setDisambigModalOpen(false);
 173:     setClinicalScanGate("not_run");
 174:     // Captured here so the async branches below use a stable value.
 175:     const clinicalQuestionOnly = template === "clinical" && uploads.length === 0;
 176:     try {
 177:       const decision = await checkScope(template, question.trim());
 178:       if (scanGenerationRef.current !== myGeneration) return; // stale — discard
 179:       setScopeDecision(decision);
 180:       if (decision.verdict === "accepted" && uploads.length > 0) {
 181:         // Upload-backed ambiguity: candidates come from document chunks.
 182:         const candidates = uploads.flatMap((u, ui) =>
 183:           u.chunk_preview.map((text, ci) => ({
 184:             source_id: `${u.document_id}:${ui}-${ci}`,
 185:             text,
 186:           })),
 187:         );
 188:         if (candidates.length > 0) {
 189:           const result = await checkAmbiguity(question.trim(), candidates);
 190:           if (scanGenerationRef.current !== myGeneration) return; // stale
 191:           setAmbiguity(result);
 192:           if (result.is_ambiguous) setDisambigModalOpen(true);
 193:         }
 194:       } else if (decision.verdict !== "rejected" && clinicalQuestionOnly) {
 195:         // Question-only clinical run: the backend fetches candidates and
 196:         // runs detect_ambiguity. A successful scan is mandatory before a
 197:         // run may start (see the onSubmit gate below).
 198:         const result = await scanAmbiguity(question.trim());
 199:         if (scanGenerationRef.current !== myGeneration) return; // stale
 200:         setAmbiguity(result);
 201:         setClinicalScanGate("ok");
 202:         if (result.is_ambiguous) setDisambigModalOpen(true);
 203:       }
 204:     } catch (err) {
 205:       if (scanGenerationRef.current !== myGeneration) return; // stale — discard
 206:       if (clinicalQuestionOnly) setClinicalScanGate("failed");
 207:       setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Scope check failed");
 208:     } finally {
 209:       // Always clear the in-progress flag — only one runScopeCheck is ever
 210:       // in flight (the button is disabled while scopeChecking).
 211:       setScopeChecking(false);
 212:     }
 213:   };
 214: 
 215:   const onSubmit = async (event: React.FormEvent) => {
 216:     event.preventDefault();
 217:     if (question.trim().length < 4) {
 218:       setError("Question must be at least 4 characters.");
 219:       return;
 220:     }
 221:     if (scopeDecision?.verdict === "rejected") {
 222:       setError("Scope gate rejected this question. Reframe before submitting.");
 223:       return;
 224:     }
 225:     // I-rdy-009 (#505): a clinical question-only run must not start unless
 226:     // the ambiguity scan succeeded. A 503, a never-run scan, a post-scan
 227:     // edit, or a discarded stale in-flight scan all leave the gate != "ok".
 228:     if (
 229:       template === "clinical" &&
 230:       uploads.length === 0 &&
 231:       clinicalScanGate !== "ok"
 232:     ) {
 233:       setError(
 234:         clinicalScanGate === "failed"
 235:           ? "Ambiguity check is unavailable — retry Check scope before starting a run."
 236:           : "Run Check scope first — the ambiguity guard must complete for clinical questions.",
 237:       );
 238:       return;
 239:     }
 240:     if (ambiguity?.is_ambiguous && !acknowledgedAmbiguity) {
 241:       setError(
 242:         "Ambiguity detected. Resolve it in the disambiguation modal before starting a run.",
 243:       );
 244:       return;
 245:     }
 246:     setSubmitting(true);
 247:     setError(null);
 248:     try {
 249:       const run = await createRun({
 250:         template,
 251:         question: question.trim(),
 252:         document_ids: uploads.map((u) => u.document_id),
 253:       });
 254:       router.push(`/runs/${run.run_id}`);
 255:     } catch (err) {
 256:       const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Unknown error";
 257:       setError(message);
 258:       setSubmitting(false);
 259:     }
 260:   };

 succeeded in 833ms:
   1: """HDBSCAN-based ambiguity detector for research questions.
   2: 
   3: Per docs/carney_delivery_plan_v6_2.md F2 (ambiguity detector backend) and
   4: memory bpei_phantom_completion_lessons.md, the BPEI failure happened
   5: because the scope gate has no way to detect when a short acronym question
   6: maps to multiple unrelated source clusters. This module fixes that by:
   7: 
   8: 1. Running a cheap candidate retrieval (top-K from search providers).
   9: 2. Embedding the candidate snippets via a deterministic encoder.
  10: 3. Clustering with HDBSCAN.
  11: 4. If ≥2 clusters meet min_cluster_size, return AmbiguityResult with
  12:    per-cluster representative snippets so the UI can render a
  13:    disambiguation modal.
  14: 
  15: Phase 0 ships the API surface + a pure-Python fallback that uses character
  16: 3-gram cosine + a simple density-based grouping when scikit-learn /
  17: hdbscan are not installed (so this code can be unit-tested without the
  18: heavy ML stack). Phase 1 wires the real HDBSCAN path once the backend
  19: venv is provisioned.
  20: """
  21: 
  22: from __future__ import annotations
  23: 
  24: import math
  25: import re
  26: from collections import Counter
  27: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
  28: from typing import Sequence
  29: 
  30: 
  31: @dataclass
  32: class CandidateSnippet:
  33:     """One candidate retrieval result feeding the disambiguation pass."""
  34: 
  35:     source_id: str
  36:     text: str
  37: 
  38: 
  39: @dataclass
  40: class AmbiguityCluster:
  41:     """A discovered semantic cluster of candidates."""
  42: 
  43:     cluster_id: int
  44:     representative_text: str
  45:     member_source_ids: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
  46: 
  47: 
  48: @dataclass
  49: class AmbiguityResult:
  50:     """Detector verdict.
  51: 
  52:     `is_ambiguous` is True iff there are ≥2 clusters each with at least
  53:     `min_cluster_size` members. Each cluster's representative snippet is
  54:     surfaced to the user via the F2 disambiguation modal.
  55:     """
  56: 
  57:     is_ambiguous: bool
  58:     clusters: list[AmbiguityCluster]
  59:     fallback_used: bool = False
  60: 
  61: 
  62: _TOKEN_RE = re.compile(r"[a-z0-9]+")
  63: 
  64: 
  65: def _trigrams(text: str) -> Counter[str]:
  66:     text_lower = text.lower()
  67:     counts: Counter[str] = Counter()
  68:     for token in _TOKEN_RE.findall(text_lower):
  69:         padded = f"  {token}  "
  70:         for i in range(len(padded) - 2):
  71:             counts[padded[i : i + 3]] += 1
  72:     return counts
  73: 
  74: 
  75: def _cosine(a: Counter[str], b: Counter[str]) -> float:
  76:     if not a or not b:
  77:         return 0.0
  78:     dot = sum(a[k] * b[k] for k in a.keys() & b.keys())
  79:     norm_a = math.sqrt(sum(v * v for v in a.values()))
  80:     norm_b = math.sqrt(sum(v * v for v in b.values()))
  81:     if norm_a == 0 or norm_b == 0:
  82:         return 0.0
  83:     return dot / (norm_a * norm_b)
  84: 
  85: 
  86: def _greedy_cluster(
  87:     snippets: Sequence[CandidateSnippet], *, similarity_threshold: float
  88: ) -> list[list[int]]:
  89:     if not snippets:
  90:         return []
  91:     grams = [_trigrams(s.text) for s in snippets]
  92:     unassigned = list(range(len(snippets)))
  93:     clusters: list[list[int]] = []
  94:     while unassigned:
  95:         seed = unassigned.pop(0)
  96:         members = [seed]
  97:         remaining: list[int] = []
  98:         for idx in unassigned:
  99:             if _cosine(grams[seed], grams[idx]) >= similarity_threshold:
 100:                 members.append(idx)
 101:             else:
 102:                 remaining.append(idx)
 103:         unassigned = remaining
 104:         clusters.append(members)
 105:     return clusters
 106: 
 107: 
 108: def detect_ambiguity(
 109:     snippets: Sequence[CandidateSnippet],
 110:     *,
 111:     min_cluster_size: int = 2,
 112:     similarity_threshold: float = 0.5,
 113:     max_clusters_surfaced: int = 4,
 114: ) -> AmbiguityResult:
 115:     """Detect whether a candidate set has ≥2 distinct semantic clusters.
 116: 
 117:     Args:
 118:         snippets: candidate retrieval snippets.
 119:         min_cluster_size: a cluster must have at least this many members
 120:             to count toward the ambiguity verdict.
 121:         similarity_threshold: trigram-cosine cutoff for the fallback
 122:             clusterer.
 123:         max_clusters_surfaced: cap on clusters returned to UI.
 124:     """
 125:     if not snippets:
 126:         return AmbiguityResult(is_ambiguous=False, clusters=[], fallback_used=True)
 127: 
 128:     raw_clusters = _greedy_cluster(snippets, similarity_threshold=similarity_threshold)
 129:     qualifying = [c for c in raw_clusters if len(c) >= min_cluster_size]
 130:     qualifying.sort(key=len, reverse=True)
 131:     qualifying = qualifying[:max_clusters_surfaced]
 132: 
 133:     out_clusters = [
 134:         AmbiguityCluster(
 135:             cluster_id=i,
 136:             representative_text=snippets[member_indices[0]].text,
 137:             member_source_ids=[snippets[idx].source_id for idx in member_indices],
 138:         )
 139:         for i, member_indices in enumerate(qualifying)
 140:     ]
 141: 
 142:     return AmbiguityResult(
 143:         is_ambiguous=len(out_clusters) >= 2,
 144:         clusters=out_clusters,
 145:         fallback_used=True,
 146:     )

 succeeded in 798ms:
   1: """GPG detached-signature signer for the bundle manifest.
   2: 
   3: Per `.codex/slices/slice_004/architecture_proposal.md` §"gpg_signer".
   4: 
   5: Wraps python-gnupg to produce a detached, ASCII-armored signature
   6: over the manifest YAML. Uses the system gpg binary; the keyring is
   7: either the OS-default (~/.gnupg) or a custom directory pointed to by
   8: GNUPGHOME env var.
   9: 
  10: Fail-loud per LAW II:
  11: - gpg binary missing → RuntimeError at construction
  12: - Signing key missing or wrong passphrase → RuntimeError with code
  13: - Signing failure → RuntimeError with surfaced gpg stderr
  14: 
  15: External verifiers run:
  16:     gpg --verify manifest.yaml.asc manifest.yaml
  17: """
  18: 
  19: from __future__ import annotations
  20: 
  21: import logging
  22: import os
  23: from dataclasses import dataclass
  24: 
  25: try:
  26:     import gnupg
  27: except ImportError as e:  # pragma: no cover
  28:     raise RuntimeError(
  29:         "python-gnupg is required for slice 004 audit-bundle GPG signing"
  30:     ) from e
  31: 
  32: 
  33: _LOG = logging.getLogger(__name__)
  34: 
  35: 
  36: @dataclass
  37: class GPGSignerConfig:
  38:     key_id: str                        # 'aldrinor@c-polarbiotech.com' or fingerprint
  39:     passphrase: str | None = None      # for non-empty key passphrase
  40:     gnupghome: str | None = None       # custom keyring dir; None = ~/.gnupg
  41:     armor: bool = True
  42: 
  43: 
  44: def load_config_from_env() -> GPGSignerConfig:
  45:     """Build config from POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID + optional POLARIS_GPG_PASSPHRASE.
  46: 
  47:     Raises RuntimeError if POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID is unset.
  48:     """
  49:     key_id = os.environ.get("POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID", "").strip()
  50:     if not key_id:
  51:         raise RuntimeError(
  52:             "POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID is required to sign audit bundles. Set it "
  53:             "in .env to a key id or fingerprint that exists in the gpg "
  54:             "keyring. Per CLAUDE.md LAW II, this MUST fail loudly."
  55:         )
  56:     passphrase = os.environ.get("POLARIS_GPG_PASSPHRASE", "").strip() or None
  57:     gnupghome = os.environ.get("GNUPGHOME", "").strip() or None
  58:     return GPGSignerConfig(
  59:         key_id=key_id,
  60:         passphrase=passphrase,
  61:         gnupghome=gnupghome,
  62:     )
  63: 
  64: 
  65: @dataclass
  66: class GPGSigner:
  67:     """Stateful signer; reuses one gnupg.GPG instance per process."""
  68: 
  69:     config: GPGSignerConfig
  70: 
  71:     def __post_init__(self):
  72:         kwargs = {}
  73:         if self.config.gnupghome:
  74:             kwargs["gnupghome"] = self.config.gnupghome
  75:         self._gpg = gnupg.GPG(**kwargs)
  76:         # Sanity check: gpg binary is callable
  77:         try:
  78:             _ = self._gpg.version
  79:         except Exception as exc:
  80:             raise RuntimeError(
  81:                 f"gpg binary unavailable or unreadable: {exc!r}"
  82:             ) from exc
  83: 
  84:     def list_secret_keys(self) -> list[dict]:
  85:         """Useful for diagnostics — what private keys can we sign with."""
  86:         return self._gpg.list_keys(secret=True)
  87: 
  88:     def sign(self, payload: bytes) -> bytes:
  89:         """Produce detached, ASCII-armored signature over `payload`.
  90: 
  91:         Returns the .asc bytes (the signature itself, not concatenated
  92:         with the payload). Raises RuntimeError on any signing failure.
  93:         """
  94:         sig = self._gpg.sign(
  95:             payload,
  96:             keyid=self.config.key_id,
  97:             passphrase=self.config.passphrase,
  98:             detach=True,
  99:             clearsign=False,
 100:             binary=not self.config.armor,
 101:         )
 102:         # python-gnupg's Sign object stringifies to the signature; check
 103:         # status to detect failures (sig.status / sig.returncode).
 104:         if not sig:
 105:             raise RuntimeError(
 106:                 f"GPG sign returned empty signature for key "
 107:                 f"{self.config.key_id!r}; status={getattr(sig, 'status', None)!r}"
 108:             )
 109:         signature = str(sig)
 110:         if "BEGIN PGP SIGNATURE" not in signature:
 111:             raise RuntimeError(
 112:                 f"GPG sign produced output without ASCII-armor headers; "
 113:                 f"likely passphrase or key issue. status="
 114:                 f"{getattr(sig, 'status', None)!r}"
 115:             )
 116:         return signature.encode("utf-8")
 117: 
 118: 
 119: def build_gpg_signer() -> GPGSigner:
 120:     """Factory: read env, instantiate signer."""
 121:     return GPGSigner(config=load_config_from_env())
